DROP DATABASE IF EXISTS `hestia`;
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS `hestia`;

USE `hestia`;

/*
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
-- Création des tables -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
*/

 

/*
# ----------------- admin -----------
*/

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS user_admin
(
	`id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT, 
	`firstname` VARCHAR(63) NOT NULL, 
 	`lastname` VARCHAR(63) NOT NULL, 
	`email` VARCHAR(63) NOT NULL, 
	`password` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
	`createdAt` DATETIME  NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW() , 
	UNIQUE ( `email`) ,
	PRIMARY KEY(`id`)
);

/*
# ----------------- agency -----------
*/

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS agency
(
	`id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT, 
	`slug` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
	`title` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
	`logo_url` VARCHAR(511) NOT NULL, 
	`createdAt` DATETIME  NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW() , 
    
	`bio` VARCHAR(2047) NOT NULL, 
	`address` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, 
	`agencyCreation` DATE NOT NULL  , 
	`encours` FLOAT  DEFAULT 0,
	`fund` BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
	`effective` INT DEFAULT 0,
	`MajorityShareholder` VARCHAR(255)  ,
	`phone` INT(10) NOT NULL ,
	`email` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, 
    
 
	UNIQUE ( `slug`) ,
	PRIMARY KEY(`id`)
);
 

 ------------- SCPI ------------------------}

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS scpi
(
	`id` INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT, 
	`createdAt` DATETIME  NOT NULL DEFAULT NOW() , 
	`parentAgency` INT NOT NULL,
	`slug` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
	`title` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, 
	`inOurSelection` BOOLEAN  DEFAULT false, 
	`lifeInsurance` BOOLEAN  DEFAULT false, 
	`type` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, 
	`category` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, 
	`localisation` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, 
    `distributionRate` FLOAT NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 ,
    `partPrice` FLOAT NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    `capitalisation` BIGINT NOT NULL,
	`scpiCreation` DATE NOT NULL  , 
    `profil` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    `history` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    `description` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
 
`capitalType` VARCHAR(255) Not NULL,
`minSub` INT Not NULL DEFAULT 1,
 
`periodOfEnjoyment` VARCHAR(255),
`subscriptionFee` FLOAT DEFAULT 0 ,
`gestionFee` FLOAT DEFAULT 0 ,
`visaAMF` VARCHAR(255),
    
		CONSTRAINT `hs_scpi`
	 FOREIGN KEY (`parentAgency`)
	  REFERENCES `agency` (`id`)
	  ON DELETE CASCADE
	  ON UPDATE RESTRICT , 

	UNIQUE ( `slug`) ,
	PRIMARY KEY(`id`)
);

--  AGENCY + SCPI -> see ./generate.js

 SELECT id , GROUP_CONCAT(SELECT * FROM scpi WHERE parentAgency= 1 ) AS COUNT 
 FROM agency 
 WHERE id = 1 
 
 ;
